  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260549516" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1836974556418735034"><b> 4 Second Chance Stars. </b>	<br/><br/>I will not say much about this book, because I believe this is one of those stories that you have to discover page by page. Let’s just say that Charlie and Jase met when they were kids. And that was the day the fell in love. But their love wasn’t perfect and wasn’t all roses and cupcakes… like real life rarely is. <br/>This story takes place in the present, when they aren’t currently together, but in takes us on a ride to the past, telling us what happened between them. And w</span>
  <span id="freeText1836974556418735034" style="display:none"><b> 4 Second Chance Stars. </b>	<br><br>I will not say much about this book, because I believe this is one of those stories that you have to discover page by page. Let’s just say that Charlie and Jase met when they were kids. And that was the day the fell in love. But their love wasn’t perfect and wasn’t all roses and cupcakes… like real life rarely is. <br>This story takes place in the present, when they aren’t currently together, but in takes us on a ride to the past, telling us what happened between them. And what will happen when life puts them in the same path again. Get in, it will be an emotional ride, but you will not regret. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430061179i/14674690.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I first saw that this book was based on real events, I knew it wasn’t going to be an easy read: it wasn’t. I’m a person who starts reading a book immediately after finishing another, yet, I didn’t read anything else because I’m with a hangover from this one.<br>Let me very honest: this is a book that I’ll never re-read. Not because I didn’t like it, I did, but because there was so much hurt, that my heart still breaks when I remember what the heroes have had to deal through life. This is an emotional reading, full of angst, where you will want to scream with the protagonists, and you’ll want to scream about how unfair life sometimes is. And when things finally start to shine, this book will make you realize that life is exactly that: learn how to deal with the bad, enjoy the good and turn it into amazing memories for when we need motivation to keep going. <br>This wasn’t, for sure, an easy reading. But it was an unforgettable one. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429744792i/14626262.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> The best part of this book was getting a change of seeing the protagonists grow, not only in age but also in character. We’ve heard their story since they were 9 years old, until the present time when they are already adults. You’re going to love them, hate them sometimes, but they aren’t flawless heroes and that is what made me like them: they were real. With fears, wrong and right decisions and feelings they didn’t know how to deal with, especially in the teenage years. You’re going to want to kick their asses, but stick with them, in the end it’ll all make sense. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Some heated moments. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Abuse. Rape. Drugs.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They are with other people through the book, but never a “real” triangle. They were never unsure of their feelings for each other.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes. With the most emotional epilogue ever, I swear I still get teary eyed when I remember it.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1917544158" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1917544158" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1917544158?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=beautiful-writing">beautiful-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=addiction">addiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=highly-recommended">highly-recommended</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=more-than-5-stars">more-than-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=physical-abuse">physical-abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=heartache">heartache</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=trigger-alert">trigger-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=rape">rape</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=deep-emotions">deep-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=drama-and-healing">drama-and-healing</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1917544158" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5151287074452015484">Joey raised his glass higher. <b>“Here’s to falling…”</b> He leveled his eyes on both of us. <b>“…in love…and to the best example of it that I’ve ever seen...” </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506456923i/24020281._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>HERE’S TO FALLING</b> is a novel inspired by the events that the writer herself has lived through...<br/><br/>The following is the author’s note at the beginning of the novel.<br/><br/><b>Author’s Note:</b><br/><br/><i>It took me over twenty years to get this story out. Little by little, over the years I wrote, trying to get everything down. My readers will probably be able to tell the diffe</i></span>
  <span id="freeText5151287074452015484" style="display:none">Joey raised his glass higher. <b>“Here’s to falling…”</b> He leveled his eyes on both of us. <b>“…in love…and to the best example of it that I’ve ever seen...” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506456923i/24020281._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>HERE’S TO FALLING</b> is a novel inspired by the events that the writer herself has lived through...<br><br>The following is the author’s note at the beginning of the novel.<br><br><b>Author’s Note:</b><br><br><i>It took me over twenty years to get this story out. Little by little, over the years I wrote, trying to get everything down. My readers will probably be able to tell the difference between the things I wrote long ago and things I wrote more recently. Honestly, this is probably the first story I really ever wrote. Trust me when I say it was very hard to do. <b>It’s inspired by events that I have lived through.</b> You’ll know the events when you read them. I weaved fiction through the story to make it a story . Just realize I’m giving you a piece of me on these pages. I hope my words are strong enough.</i><br><br>And knowing this is what makes it 10 times more painful and real when you read it.<br><br><b>HERE'S TO FALLING</b> is one of the most painful life stories I have read. I don’t know which parts were fiction but even one trauma in the book is more than enough for someone in a lifetime. <br><br>So, I really would like to thank Ms. Zolendz for creating such a magnificent book out of the equally beautiful &amp; painful experiences of her own life. <br><br><b>HERE’S TO FALLING</b> will make your heart melt at the unique friendship of Joey, Jase and Charlotte (aka Charlie)... <br>But it will also crush your heart because of their sufferings. <br><br>All in all, it is worth the pain and the book is a must-read, if you ask me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019182._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Writing:</b><br><br>It is difficult to write your own life experiences and create a novel out of it. Ms. Zolendz does it skillfully. The writing of the book is really very good. It keeps you hooked. It goes back to the childhood and teenage years of these three close friends, and comes back to the present. So it is a time travel between present and past all the time.<br><br>It is told by two main characters, Charlie &amp; Jase and this dual point of view is my favorite as it lets me know what both sides think and feel.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446925i/24019210._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Content:</b><br><br>There is a beautiful story of friendship in it.<br>There is a heart-felt love story in it.<br>There is a great amount of happiness in it.<br>But...<br>There are also evil people in it.<br>There is a lot of pain and suffering in it.<br>More importantly, there are many triggers in it.<br>Still, it is worth all the suffering, and I say, "do read it".<br><br>This book had also many of my triggers in it. Normally, I finish reading a book in one or two days but this took me a much longer time (more than a week) because I couldn’t bear the suffering in it, so I gave long breaks after each chapter or two. I needed to put the book aside for a while and collect some more courage before starting it again.<br><br>I remember going to bed, crying for them and falling into sleep with tears in my eyes. I thanked God for my own tragedies when I read about theirs. I won't complain ever again!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019191._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>About the events &amp; triggers:</b><br><br>I always write about the triggers and include warnings of safety in my reviews... But not this time. This will be my exception.<br><br>I don’t want to say much and spoil it, so I won’t go into many details. I won’t write the triggers as a spoiler even by hiding them because the truth is if I had known about those triggers, I wouldn’t have read this book but now I don’t regret a bit having read it no matter how much it pained me. <br><br>Therefore, I am now, on purpose, avoiding to inform you about the triggers because I know when I write them, they may cause you to avoid the book but the book is too good to avoid because of these triggers, it is a must-read, if you ask me.<br><br>So, whenever you feel courageous enough for a heart-felt story that might break your heart but then put it back together, go read this book. It is highly recommended. (Or, pm me if you really need to know about these triggers.)<br><br>The book shows the ugly sides of life, the bad side of some people - to the maximum extent of their evilness - and it also shows the weaknesses of others. It is a fiction based on real life so expect real life beauty and real life ugliness in it. It is not a light and fun book, not a pink-colored story. Not everything that happens in it is what we expect in our romance books. Ugly things happen here. Painful things happen here. And everyone deals with their trauma in a different way. But it still contains something very beautiful in it - a pure friendship and a deep love story.<br><br>I have read some very negative reviews about this book and I must say that nothing is as it seems in the negative reviews. You need to read and see yourself what caused them to make these mistakes because everything is in the details and you need to know these details to understand the characters' actions...<br><br><b>This is not a love triangle</b> between best friends... Nope, not at all! This is completely a different story... Life ripping apart three best friends, two of whom were lovers.<br><br>Here are some quotes that may help you decide...<br><br><b>
  <i>The heat from his body up against mine, the smell of the shampoo he used, the press of his lips against mine, and there was nothing and no one else in the world, but us. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506446845ra/24019188.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>JUMPING DOWN THE RABBIT HOLE</b><br><br><b>
  <i>In my head, the written words of Lewis Carroll whispered in my ears, “In another moment, down went Alice after it, never once considering how in the world she was to get out again.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407972ra/797505.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506446845ra/24019186.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>Jase didn’t kiss me again after our seven minutes in Heaven, and we never spoke about it. <br>But sometimes… sometimes, I would catch those blue eyes on me, and when I did… <br>I would look right back at him. <br>And he never looked away.<br><br>***<br><br>There are sad songs that no one should ever have to listen to. <br>Goodbyes that no one should ever say. <br>Life is messy, it's never fair, and it's never pretty. <br><br>And I will always ask God why, why, why, why?<br>And I'll never get an answer. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506450384i/24019719._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>All around us, people were going on, living, breathing, working, laughing; whatever it was they did. But, we noticed nothing. None of it mattered, because we were the world to each other. Our kisses healed our tears. Our touches healed our sadness, and we healed each other. There was nothing that could ever come between us. We were each other’s forever. <br><br>But forever isn’t real. Is it?</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1506446845ra/24019181.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>MEMORIES OF THE TREE-HOUSE</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446859i/24019196._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>In the space between now and then, before and after, there’s a lifetime. A lifetime of the choices you could have made, the paths you choose at the forks in the road, and the paths you never took. <br><br>It’s a lifetime full of wondering who you truly are or who you could have been if you had just taken that other path.<br><br>Sometimes, I cry so hard. Sometimes I scream so loud, just wishing for that heartbroken seventeen-year-old girl to take a different path. <br><br>But, she doesn’t hear me.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019187._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019183._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I tried to forget. I tried to forget how everything happened, how the whole damn Charlie-Joey-fuck-my-life-situation played out. About how I tried getting it all back, but I couldn’t bring back shit.<br><br>Sometimes, when I’m working, and I see a woman with that long, silky chestnut colored hair standing in a crowd, my body freezes, and I stare at her until I know for sure it isn’t Charlie. <br><br>It’s never Charlie. <br><br>No one had that cinnamon colored hair; nobody held a cigarette the same way Charlie did. <br>Nobody ever had a book clenched tightly to her chest, and nobody’s laugh sounded anything like hers. <br>And no one ever looked at me the way Charlie did. <br>It had been years, and no one had ever come close to being anything like Charlie. <br><br>And Joey, well that was a whole other different level of shit. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019184._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"He's talking about you, Detective." I enunciated every word clearly and curtly. <br>The room stilled–quieted for a few heartbeats. Everyone was watching me. <br>"Pardon me?" <br>"He sees when I text you."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019190._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446859i/24019197._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506446845i/24019189._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506449628i/24019615._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>The words hung in the air. <br>Heavy with implications. <br>After what seemed like an interminable silence, Jase's entire body stiffened, his head turned, and his wide-open gaze slowly locked onto mine. <br>"Charlie..." <br>"Charlie? " <br>As if I physically hit him, he staggered back, his head slowly shaking with its denial. His face blanched to a sickening white, and his stare turned vacant. Immediately, his brain put the pieces together and he just knew.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506450173i/24019661._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>His fingertips touched my face as tears slid down his cheeks. I'd never in my life seen a grown man cry. A fire spread across my chest and pooled up into my throat. I wanted to cover my face, curl up into a ball, and die, but he needed this. He needed to see me and forget all we ever were. <br>"No, Charlie. No, no. No, please, no." <br>He fell to his knees in front of me. <br>"How do I take that back? How? How do I erase that?"<br><br>***<br><br>"I can't leave you like this. I can't leave us like this," I whispered. <br>"Like what?" <br>"Unfinished."</i>
</b><br><br>5 stars from the bottom of my heart. This story will always stay with me...<br><br>(<i>
  <b>Not recommended to those who need safety in books but I must add that the book is worth all the pain it causes.</b>
</i>)<br><br>P.S. Note to writer &amp; publisher: I would definitely prefer a cover with 3 of them! Please change the present cover that doesn't say anything about the novel itself!</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12180287-ab?shelf=slow-burn-baby">slow-burn-baby</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1250980635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1405612626859101396">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br/><br/><b>Now LIVE!<br/>Amazon - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1Dlm3Bs'>http://amzn.to/1Dlm3Bs</a><br/>Amazon UK - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1Hk5onD'>http://amzn.to/1Hk5onD</a></b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428770323i/14480677._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When a book starts off with the author telling you that the story was inspired by true events, then you know it's going to be a passionate and emotional ride. I only rate a book 5 stars if it hits me in the gut and this one did, massively.<br/><br/>The blurb is vague, and I think it is vague for a reason. This story is best read blind so my review will contain few details as to the actual story.<br/>_ _ _ _<br/><br/>Charlie Sto</span>
  <span id="freeText1405612626859101396" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars</b> ★★★★★<br><br><b>Now LIVE!<br>Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Dlm3Bs">http://amzn.to/1Dlm3Bs</a><br>Amazon UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Hk5onD">http://amzn.to/1Hk5onD</a></b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428770323i/14480677._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When a book starts off with the author telling you that the story was inspired by true events, then you know it's going to be a passionate and emotional ride. I only rate a book 5 stars if it hits me in the gut and this one did, massively.<br><br>The blurb is vague, and I think it is vague for a reason. This story is best read blind so my review will contain few details as to the actual story.<br>_ _ _ _<br><br>Charlie Stone is a twenty four year old tattoo artist, living in New York City. She is in a bad relationship with a man called Bren who treats her badly and she is seriously starting to doubt why she is still with him. She is resigned to never finding true love again, having lost it when she was seventeen.<br><br>We flit from past to present, flawlessly I might add, and we are introduced to a younger and more innocent and happy Charlie who has two best friends, Joey and Jase.<br><br>The innocence and loyalty that the three of them experience was a joy to read, and we journey with them right up until they turn 17.<br><br>As with life, the older you get, the more jaded you become and it kicks you in the face just when things are on the up.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428771350i/14480725._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This is a story about love and friendship, and second chances.<br>_ _ _ _<br><br>This was not a love triangle but as with most teenage trials and tribulation it comes with a little angst so be prepared to want to shout at the characters to sort themselves out. I loved the sexual tension, and the hero was a true sweetheart, I loved him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"What do you say, Charlie? Want to try jumping down the rabbit hole again?<br>I promise I'll be better than any adventure you could ever read.<br>The way I see it, Charlie, is that you've always belonged to me."</b>
</blockquote><br>Charlie was a great character, feisty and fun in her younger years but very different as an adult due to her past which was understandable.<br><br>For the first half of the book, I was unsure as to how everything would all come together and I was glued to my kindle trying to work out how everybody fit in and where it was leading. When I hit the second half, boom - I was an emotional mess. It was a really beautiful story and it all came together so nicely. <br><br>I really did love this one, and considering I didn't even know it was coming out until the day I received it on my kindle, it was the best surprise.<br><br><b>This is a standalone novel, told in dual POV, but predominantly from the POV of Heroine. </b><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228252.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.facebook.com/ilovebooklove" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228250.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.twitter.com/ilovebooklove" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228251.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1264915570" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5443515700231289996"><b>2 Stars because it was apparently inspired by true events and I am sure it was hard work to write this book! <br/><br/>WARNING,...This review contains a lot of spoilers as a reflection of my own frustration and misery with the whole experience of this book! I am not, however, discouraging anyone from reading this book. This is merely my own opinion and I wish the author the best in her writing future, she really does have a way to tell the story, its just not for me.</b><br/><br/>I finally finished the book, but what i</span>
  <span id="freeText5443515700231289996" style="display:none"><b>2 Stars because it was apparently inspired by true events and I am sure it was hard work to write this book! <br><br>WARNING,...This review contains a lot of spoilers as a reflection of my own frustration and misery with the whole experience of this book! I am not, however, discouraging anyone from reading this book. This is merely my own opinion and I wish the author the best in her writing future, she really does have a way to tell the story, its just not for me.</b><br><br>I finally finished the book, but what it left me was a whole new matter!.. My mind is completely exhausted and brained washed from all the abuse and trauma associated with the experience...I am not joking, there were so many bad things happening in this book..one after another and there was very little romance in it...it was all suffering and humiliation and my head was spinning in a massive headage from all this drama!<br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/giphy_zpsbipucknf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448406976ra/17134747.gif" alt=" photo giphy_zpsbipucknf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>This book is categorised as a "romance" so for christ sake give me that romance!!! But there was very little there...the hero and heroine have not actually met <b>until 77%...</b> and all I was reading were some childhood memories of their friendship with another character that later was no longer there with them <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[died <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>...and I am scratching my head...<b>WHAT WAS THE PURPOSE OF THIS BOOK?...</b> I am not saying the childhood memories of them being together were bad, they were actually very engaging and beautiful in some parts and I understood the author's purpose was to show "how strong of a connection" Hero and heroine shared together and how they had fallen in love with each other, but later in the middle..the childhood memories turned into something entirely different and become a nightmare that lasted 77% of the book...<br> <a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/tumblr_mamp2toedK1qclb0e_zpsyjfdkyhj.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448406976ra/17134748.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mamp2toedK1qclb0e_zpsyjfdkyhj.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>They all had a messed up and heartbreaking childhood that was depressing enough, but NO the author had to dig deeper and the reader was confronted with many sexually explicit scene that were just pure torture...nothing to do with a romance and they have not even met yet at that point after the separation!!!<br><br>Hero loved the heroine but would not admit it to the heroine, the same goes for her and I was screaming at them <b>FOR GOODNESS SAKE! JUST ADMIT TO EACH OTHER THE TRUTH..WHY DO YOU TORTURE EACH OTHER LIKE THAT???...</b> I was sick and tired of them being with other people, <b>SO THEY LOVED EACH OTHER, BUT THEY WOULD NOT WANT TO BE CLOSE, BUT THEY DID NOT MIND THAT WITH COMPLETELY STRANGE PEOPLE???...And the list just goes on....</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>1.</b> Heroine went out to a party with another boy and the Hero got angry with her for doing it, but why? He said nothing to her, not admitted anything that he loves her and hey PAY BACK! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>Heroine saw him shortly after with another girl kissing her...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>But all I saw was Jase kissing Rachel Jenson up against the side of his house. I knew without a doubt how trapped my heart was in his hands, the minute his lips left hers to call out, “Have fun Charlotte Stone! And, hey! Mason, make sure you kiss her real good, I double dog dare you!”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And in that very moment, she realised that she was in love with him? WOW Isn't that romantic to see a guy you love kissing another woman? Hey but the torture just started! <br><br><b>2.</b> For over a year...they were with other people...watching kissing others and in other episodes the Hero had a sexual encounter and heroine saw him coming out of the corner with another woman with an open shirt and unbuttoned jeans...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>Dropping his hands off the giggling girl, he swayed toward me and laughed in my face. “Really, Charlie? I just got me a nice little birthday blowjob from Kylie over here. You up for giving me a better one?</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Yeah, he loves her but having one with a girl means nothing....<br><br>Heroine asking about it later <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>“I forgot about Kylie the minute I zipped up my pants.”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>The visual was enough to make me feel...<br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/annie-gagging_zpsa04n2ww6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443647095ra/16388901.gif" alt=" photo annie-gagging_zpsa04n2ww6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>3.</b> After separation the Hero was having casual sex with a woman (his coworker) and spend 3 nights with her having sex with her and there were details of her doing sexual things to him, but when she started, kissing and licking <b>THE VERY NAME OF THE HEROINE TATTOOED ON HIS heart</b> I literally felt such violation to the very love he felt for her! That tattoo was a sacred name and place for the Hero, as it represented their undying love for each other...<br><i>"That Christmas we exchanged silver rings and vowed to never love anyone but each other. For Valentine’s Day, we got fake IDs that said we were eighteen, so we could get half-heart tattoos. When we held hands, it made one heart."</i><br><br>I don't know, but him allowing a woman he did not even love licking that name? I was feeling very uncomfortable reading it and the visual stayed with me for the rest of the book! <br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/tumblr_m7eq4t1nb31rziwwco1_1280_zpsxbbafldn.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427602725ra/14293288.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m7eq4t1nb31rziwwco1_1280_zpsxbbafldn.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>4.</b> Heroine also had a boyfriend after separation and there were references to them having sex and how she did it with him...Man do I want the detail how the heroine have sex? Again is this a romance between hero and heroine? because to me it looks like its about their life with other people! <br><b>5.</b> WARNING! Heroine went through something horrifying and again I was subjected to it...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Explicitaly detailed rape scene with Heroes father and her having an orgasm/even that she hated it <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Do I want to read this, worst knowing who the person is? I felt disgusted and I don't think i should feel like that..reading a romance and being subjected to so many degrading situation..WHERE IS THE LIGH HERE? I still need some happiness..but NO another coffin came in the form of the Heroes emails after separation....<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"Charlie Okay so today I’m writing to tell you that I fucked another girl. Yep. I just went there. I hope you’re having just as much fun as I am. Jase"<br><br>"Charlie Happy anniversary of the day you fucking broke my heart. I guess that’s a little too harsh maybe. Nah, fuck you. Fuck you. I’m in the Middle East watching my friends die, and you fucking left me. You left me without any fucking clue."<br><br>"Charlie, Last night I fucked two girls. Two girls at the same time. But you don't care, do you? I hate that between the two of them, it was you I thought about."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br>OMG...I thought my heart would broke for the heroine..I know she wanted to separate herself from him due to what happened to her, but that fact did not made me happy..it still made be suffer reading it...<br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/tumblr_nqglhyNzK11urj5ilo8_400_zpsurfxslfm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448406976ra/17134749.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_nqglhyNzK11urj5ilo8_400_zpsurfxslfm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Thinking that nightmare would soon end, I was delusional...after finally meeting each other at 77% Hero was treating the heroine like some unworthy human being that does not deserve dignity and respect! <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>."You were my world, Charlie. Losing you killed me." Push her. Make her break. My chest was ready to explode. "But all along you were nothing more than where you came from. You took right after your parents, didn't you? Just like your mother, who'd fuck anything for a good time. And just like your father, abandoning anything that was ever good in your life."</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Again is this a romance I am reading? does people who are each others soulmates speak to each other like that? <br><br>But hey...the author would not finish it with another romantic gesture...<br><br>At about 94% Heroine at the Heroes apartment: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>"Then, her eyes landed on the pair of pink lace panties on the top of the laundry basket, and a tight, straight smile slashed across her face.</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Was that not a beautiful gesture to have given to the both characters that suffered so much throughout the book and not even having met for 77% and having the heroine finding some panties of his random hook up? Would the author not think that they deserve more meaningful moments with each other that would cement their deep love for each other? At 77% it's hard to believe in their undying love when confronted with these very unhelpful and meaningless interactions with each other...<br><br>In the end I felt no joy when finishing the book and my brain felt like it was brained washed for all that time and I wish for this to be only...<br><a href="http://s875.photobucket.com/user/jakubowsa/media/large_zpsjty7ch0p.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448406976ra/17134750.gif" alt=" photo large_zpsjty7ch0p.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Safe Gang: No safe<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Hero and heroine were sexually with others during childhood period:...sleeping with others on separation: very graphic detailed rape scene, sexual stuff with OW/OM <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1258811155" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1258811155" />
    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1258811155?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=fab-writing">fab-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=must-reads">must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=second-chance-love">second-chance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=romance-swoon">romance-swoon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1258811155" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5924768841136664582"><b>5 hard Fallen Stars</b><br/><br/>I have yet to read a book by Christine Zolendz that hasn't rocked me, but for me this was her best...my 2015 favorite...the book that worked in every aspect. <br/><br/><b>"...one day you'll feel like your world is crashing, spinning out of control, whatever the Hell that is to you, whatever storm that comes, whatever tragedy floods your life....believe me we all get touched by some tragedy in our lives."</b><br/><br/>There is no exception for 3 young kids...three boys and one girl living to the best of </span>
  <span id="freeText5924768841136664582" style="display:none"><b>5 hard Fallen Stars</b><br><br>I have yet to read a book by Christine Zolendz that hasn't rocked me, but for me this was her best...my 2015 favorite...the book that worked in every aspect. <br><br><b>"...one day you'll feel like your world is crashing, spinning out of control, whatever the Hell that is to you, whatever storm that comes, whatever tragedy floods your life....believe me we all get touched by some tragedy in our lives."</b><br><br>There is no exception for 3 young kids...three boys and one girl living to the best of their abilities while their environment and circumstances of growing up. Misfits? Misunderstood? Perhaps....or maybe just three kids who don't conform to the norm...who find support and love among only each other. To the outside word they were the average teens...the easy targets...within their world of 3 they were everything!<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1429633799608_zpsnnhjrbid.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429664768i/14618987.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1429633799608_zpsnnhjrbid.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>We were all friends…until we weren’t.<br>We depended on each other…until we couldn’t.<br>We were in love…until we were ripped apart.<br>We moved on…even when we didn’t want to let go.</b><br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/805ca16c-c850-4c55-9fcb-09080a788884_zpsdiqu0ahc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429665982i/14619093.jpg" alt=" photo 805ca16c-c850-4c55-9fcb-09080a788884_zpsdiqu0ahc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is a read full of feels. This is a coming of age and all the humor and horror accompanied with growing up. This is the development of forever friendship and deep rooted bonds that are unbreakable between Charlie and her boys Jase and Joey. This is all the first time feelings of drink, of touch, of pleasure and of pain. This is the highs and lows of love that bloomed between Charlie and Jase. This is also the loss of innocence...the loss of self...the loss of life.<br><br><b>"I've heard people say that what you remember is not the whole truth; it's our thoughts of what we wanted things to be remembered as"</b><br><br>Life for Charlie...Joey...Jase...was best lived when together. Laughs were the loudest. Jokes were he funniest. Love was the purest. When life as they know it was no more...they ceased to exist together. Time gone by and paths led away from the heart of them all. Not a day passed when the thought of those firsts weren't constants for Charlie and Jase. No time, distance or person could sever the love that was, even when the ugliest of events shattered them.<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1429634930347_zpsrngzkn7t.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429664768i/14618989._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1429634930347_zpsrngzkn7t.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>From this young adult story, the author uses past memories and dual POVs to transition to a harsh tale if survival, poor circumstances and a never ending sadness that haunts the characters. But just as fate brought and tore the connections apart...those harsh life circumstances work to find the loss and continue the tale....and well...Here's to Falling...again!!!<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1429635021669_zpsckb6ko3z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429664768i/14618990.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1429635021669_zpsckb6ko3z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I cannot say loud enough how hard I loved this. From the young adult tale to the new adult growth I found all of my favorites for a perfect read...angst and heart wrenching sadness...frustrating emotions of anger and then overwhelming comfort and relief. This had Lol fun times and sweet sentiments that turned into sassy dialogue and raw intimacy. Christine Zolendz wrote a perfect book for me and I will praise her name for a long time!<br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5924768841136664582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer15840909377520278663">Here’s the thing, you want to read a book that makes you forget, a book that consumes you, a book that literally rocks your world. This is that book for you. My heart is still on the last page of this book... and i'm not sure if i'm getting it back.<br/><br/>I’m going to be vague in this review as going into this book blind is absolutely the way you need to go. I did. You aren’t going to find many reviews that say much about what happens or who it happens to, you need to experience it, live it!!! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499949560i/23283511._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Just kno</span>
  <span id="freeText15840909377520278663" style="display:none">Here’s the thing, you want to read a book that makes you forget, a book that consumes you, a book that literally rocks your world. This is that book for you. I did. A love that is trusting, its forgiving, and it is absolutely shattering. In a very good way!!! One that will stay with me for a really long time <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499950845ra/23283718.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260038969" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2539884677323987602"><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=210gcpi' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429652657i/14617638._SX540_.jpg' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

</a><br/><br/><b>TITLE:</b> Here's to Falling<br/><b>AUTHOR:</b> Christine Zolendz<br/><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br/><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> April 19th 2015<br/><b>MY RATING: ★★★★★</b> (I wish there were 10 stars I could give this book)<br/><br/><b>5 MY BEAUTIFUL ALIEN MONSTER STARS</b><br/><br/>Gah not far in, it's funnily sweet, the feels, I'm loving this already!! <br/><br/><i>We were all friends…until we weren’t.<br/>We depended on each other…until we couldn’t.<br/>We were in love…until we were ripped apart.<br/>We moved on…even when we didn’t want to let go.</i><br/><br/><b>This book was inspired "By True Events"</b> <br/><br/><i>C</i></span>
  <span id="freeText2539884677323987602" style="display:none"><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=210gcpi" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429652657i/14617638._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2j0jcs1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429652657i/14617639._SY540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> Here's to Falling<br><b>AUTHOR:</b> Christine Zolendz<br><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>RELEASE DATE:</b> April 19th 2015<br><b>MY RATING: ★★★★★</b> (I wish there were 10 stars I could give this book)<br><br><b>5 MY BEAUTIFUL ALIEN MONSTER STARS</b><br><br>Gah not far in, it's funnily sweet, the feels, I'm loving this already!! <br><br><i>We were all friends…until we weren’t.<br>We depended on each other…until we couldn’t.<br>We were in love…until we were ripped apart.<br>We moved on…even when we didn’t want to let go.</i><br><br><b>This book was inspired "By True Events"</b> <br><br><i>Come on, Charlie, come with me down the rabbit hole</i><br><br>And then I hit the bit that made it all seem so real, from three friends, to two..That just brutally broke my heart, just ripped my heart out and tore it to shreds, the feels are of my heart breaking in half..<br><br><i>Remember I told you about my</i> <b>BOOM</b>..<i>That was my first one..It wrecked me..My next</i> <b>BOOM,</b> <i>it completely destroyed me.</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=29fxe1c" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429652657ra/14617640.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am not a crier, but I had tears falling down my face..<b>HERE'S TO FALLING</b> like a sinking boat without a life raft..<br><br><i>We were each others FOREVER</i><br><br><b>TURN BACK</b>- Don't go!! - Run - <b>TRIGGER WARNING</b> - Gut wrenchingly raw..<b>BOOM!! HERE'S TO FALLING!!</b> <br><br><i>I was violated, defiled and utterly destroyed, it shredded me into fine, little pieces of thin tissue paper</i><br><br><b>I NEED MY BEST FRIEND</b><br><br>I'm kind of writing this rough review as I read the book, usually I can handle the raw, emotional books, I'm usually like bring it, but this book is the exception to the rule, I couldn't carry on, I had to get up make myself a coffee and then carry on with it, this book just threw those punches, a gripping tale spoken from a young eight year old as she moves through the ages, the path she took at seventeen changed not one life but two forever..<br><br><b>TWO WORLD'S COLLIDE</b> <br><br><i>True love ALWAYS comes BACK</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=e87n2q" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429653605ra/14617747.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A roller coaster of an emotional ride with twists and turns of two souls entwined..even though this is an emotionally raw book it's beautiful in its entirety..how ironic to laugh my ass off at the beginning of this book only to turn around and be crying at the end of it..<br><br><i>You've always belonged to me.</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mry4x0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429655303ra/14617969.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>He claimed my</i> <b>body</b>, <i>my</i> <b>soul</b>, <i>my</i> <b>mind</b>, <i>he claimed all of</i> <b>me</b><br><br>There are no words to convey my absolute hate for these two spineless mothers in this book!! <br><br>This book ripped my heart out and put it back together piece by piece..<br><br>This book broke me, it made me laugh, it made me cry, it made me fall in love with the story line, the characters, the writing, it also deserves to be on my favourites shelf in here..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=k36haw" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1429653605ra/14617748.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>"Here's to Falling"</b> destroyed me, it broke my heart into little pieces, I cried, I laughed and then I cried again..The feels just kept coming and coming, thank you for giving us a little piece of you..I wish I was an author and I could convey my emotions better and write a fitting review because this book just made me feel everything you set out to make me feel!! (Thank you) xxx (Kat)</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying">i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1249294892" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1425056753587529735"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502656._SX540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><br/>This was a story like nothing I have read before. It was truly a rollercoaster ride of emotions. Christine has this insane ability to make you bawl, then laugh so hard, and then make you want to put the book down and just sob on the floor. And, by the way, I did all of these. I laughed, I cried, and I even had to put the book down and just collect myself at one point. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502657._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Here's To Falling tells the story and life of Charlotte "Charlie" Stone, and her two best friends, Joey and Jase. I don't want </span>
  <span id="freeText1425056753587529735" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502656._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>This was a story like nothing I have read before. It was truly a rollercoaster ride of emotions. Christine has this insane ability to make you bawl, then laugh so hard, and then make you want to put the book down and just sob on the floor. And, by the way, I did all of these. I laughed, I cried, and I even had to put the book down and just collect myself at one point. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502657._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Here's To Falling tells the story and life of Charlotte "Charlie" Stone, and her two best friends, Joey and Jase. I don't want to give too much away about where this leads or any of the plot because apart of the thrill for me while reading was trying to figure out the mysteries entwined through out the story - Who does Charlie refer to when speaking of heartbreak? Who is she texting in the present? What happened to her friendship with Joey and Jase?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502658._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But I will say just when I thought it was going one way....BAM....I was thrown off the damn roller coaster with my jaw dropped on the floor. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502659._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>A love story at its core, but it was SO MUCH MORE than that. The journey Charlie went through is something I don’t think I will ever forget. Her strength, her courage, and more importantly, Christine’s courage to write this story is awe-inspiring. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502660._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>A slow build to an incredible story, but my god, when you reach that high point, you can’t help but fall in love with the whole thing, EVERY LAST PART, even the incredibly sad ones.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428934574i/14502661._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1445745085" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1445745085" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582366251p2/21803154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1445745085?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Definitely Everyone.</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=beautiful-stories">beautiful-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=ebooks-ibooks">ebooks-ibooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=great-fighting-scenes">great-fighting-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=childhood-friends-turn-lovers">childhood-friends-turn-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=happy-ending">happy-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=highly-recommend">highly-recommend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=realism">realism</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=will-reread">will-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=deserve-more-readers">deserve-more-readers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1445745085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14550993797163382540"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>”Come on, Charlie, come with me down the rabbit hole,” he squeaked in an unsteady voice.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br/>For starters, this is the best book I’ve read this year so far and it's also one of my top favorite NA novels. The story takes the whole NA genre up a notch and shows me that these books aren’t just about graphic sex scenes but incredibly emotional elements as well. <b>It’s a bit inappropriate to say I <i>enjoy</i> reading the book a lot because of certain reasons and background, but I’m deeply captivated </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14550993797163382540" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>”Come on, Charlie, come with me down the rabbit hole,” he squeaked in an unsteady voice.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> <br />For starters, this is the best book I’ve read this year so far and it's also one of my top favorite NA novels. The story takes the whole NA genre up a notch and shows me that these books aren’t just about graphic sex scenes but incredibly emotional elements as well. <b>It’s a bit inappropriate to say I <i>enjoy</i> reading the book a lot because of certain reasons and background, but I’m deeply captivated by its plot and the protagonists’ experiences.</b> However, I would’ve loved the book more <b>without the epilogue.</b><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Main Characters</b>
</u><br />• <b>Charlotte “Charlie” Stone</b>-<i>Before 16</i>, she had 2 best friends in the world and fell in love with one of them. <i>Before 17</i>, everything was perfectly perfect. <i>After 17</i>, she had nothing. No friends, no family, nowhere to go, and nowhere to live. There was no Charlotte Stone, either. She disappeared. She changed. She turned into a desperate damsel in distress and later worked in half of her tattoo parlor which initially owned by the third person she trusted. <i>Now 24</i>, her once settled world is turned upside down again. Everything won’t be the same, but it’s not necessarily getting worse, right?<br /><br />• <b>Jase “JD” Delaney</b>-<i>At 9</i>, he flipped Charlie off because he had no clue how to react when seeing a pretty girl. <i>At 14</i>, he was coward enough to let the girl he’d ever loved go to the dance with some jerk. <i>At 16</i>, he finally manned up and got back his girl. <i>At 17</i>, he left her involuntarily but at the same time, lost her completely. He might as well lost the largest piece of his heart to her. <i>Now 24,</i> things change and he’s a narcotic detective so the situations get complicated. <br /><br />• <b>Joey Graley</b>-He’d been Charlie's bestest best friend for as long as I know and his friendship with Charlie was definitely the ultimate goal in the entire friendship kingdom. He protected her, stood out for her, and was probably the only person who knew her jokes. Oh, and he was also the catalyst for Charlie and Jase’s relationship. Ain’t he just an awesome sauce? <br /><br /><u>
  <b>Plot</b>
</u><br />As a 24-year-old girl, Charlie tells her story by reminiscing her childhood, teenage life, and everything before that horrific night. She also lets us know how she has been in the past seven years—years without Jase and friends and family—as a result, Charlie literally becomes my close friend after I finished reading this book. All I can say about Charlie is that she’s come a long way since she endured all those inhumane things and that it’s difficult for her to tell us her story. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>A kaleidoscope of fleshy images and pain spun a design of madness before my eyes.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />To begin with, Charlie, Jase, and Joey have been besties since forever; they go to the same schools, have the same enemies, and get the same sense of humor. When they’re not hanging around in Charlie or Joey’s house, they’ll gather in Charlie’s treehouse. Ironically, that treehouse turns out to be their safe haven when they grow up, but that’s another story. <br /><br />One day, Charlie is bullied by her classmates, <b>Slate Marshall</b> and his minions in particular, because of her precocious puberty while Joey is bullied because he’s mistaken as Charlie's boyfriend. (Stupid reason, I know) Then, here comes the superhero, Jase, who has the guts to fight Slate back and defends Charlie bravely. After the incident, the undefeatable threesome has formed. <s>Adorably, since Charlie is a huge bibliophile (just like us!), she makes Jase like reading as well.</s> Throughout their early teenage years, their friendship remains as perfect as it used to be. Undoubtedly, they go on the same adventure together and explore the world in their <i>rabbit hole</i>.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>Joey read the phrase with a raised brow. “What’s Rabbit Hole mean?”<br />Jases’s eyes grazed past Joey and landed on mine. “From <i>Alice’s Adventures in Wonderland</i>, you know…down the rabbit hole, where there’s a whole different world. And it’s only ours. Our safe place to go from the jerks like Slate.”</b>
</blockquote><br />Never do they expect something tragic will happen when they’re 16, and sadly, they’re no longer the threesome. In spite of the stone cold reality, their last toast together will always stay with them/us no matter how cruel Karma is.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Then Joey raised his glass higher. “Here’s to falling…” He leveled his eyes on both of us. “…in love…and to the best example of it that I’ve ever seen, which is sitting right in front of me. And here’s to hoping my two best friends finally find the guts to tell each other they’ve been in love with one another since the fourth fucking grade. Cheers.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />Apparently, Jase and Charlie fall in love and become the most lovable couple in the entire history of coupledom. However, Jase is left kicking and screaming when he’s forced to leave Charlie. Later, Charlie experiences her biggest BOOM in her life and has forever changed. Her eyes has turned lifeless, her body used and broken, and her soul rotten.<br /><br />At the age of 24, the secret she tries so hard to protect and hide from Jase is threatened to be spilt out loud and at that moment, she knows all those sweet memories will be tarnished by the ugly truth.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>Features (WHY YOU NEED TO READ THE BOOK)</b>
</u><br />Speaking of the special features in this book, well, prepare yourself, it’s gonna be a long list (why, the book is legit!). Besides, these are also what you could expect from the book.<br /><br />✔️<b>Precious friendship.</b>: As you may know by now, Charlie, Jase, and Joey’s friendship is the best kind we can only hope for in life (or blissful enough to have one). They’ve been friends since childhood and you could see how <u>naturally it’s developed</u> from their interactions and convos.<br /><br />✔️<b>#RelationshipGoal</b>: Charlie and Jase’s relationship is <u>slowly built up</u> and they didn’t be with each other without many obstacles. Thus, challenge after challenge, they prove that their love will last for a long time, if not forever. I can’t say I don’t swoon over their steamy scenes, but I feel like cherishing them carefully because those moments are hard earned and delicate like a fragile piece of art. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>The last thing I remembered hearing was Jase’s low whisper against my ear, “Stay in the rabbit hole with me this time.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />✔️<b>BASED ON TRUE EVENTS:</b> This is probably what makes the story more relatable and convincing compared to others. The author mentions that this story takes her over 20 years to finish and finally publish, so I could feel her words through every chapter and every scene. Besides, this background also manages to make the story all the more heart-wrenching. <b>There were several times my chest convulsed with sobs while tears wouldn’t stop streaming down my face and blurring my vision and I couldn’t read the next lines.</b> The pain is excruciating and I seriously don’t understand how emotionally wrecked a person can be. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>All this time, she just went on thinking that the monster that did this was still out there, but her only worry was about how it would <i>affect me if I found out.</i> All this time I’d wanted to be her hero, and she was already mine.</b>
</blockquote><br />✔️<b>Unique layout of the TIMELINE</b>: Since the author spent more than 20 years to write this story, it’s not hard to tell the difference between her earlier parts and later ones. Although some readers find it confusing to sort out the plot line, I’m positive that once you’re used to the certain pattern of her writing style, you’ll be addicted to it. For example, you’ll realize that <b>each chapter starts with the character’s (either Charlie or Jase) current status and always ends with a piece of their childhood memory.</b> Moreover, the story is told in the chronological order; therefore, (take Charlie’s POV for example) it’s like 24(yo)→9→24→10→24→…→17→24~present.<br /> <br />✔️<b>Alternative POVs</b>: Most of the chapters are told from Charlie’s POV and some are Jase’s. Either way, they make the plot more clear and easy to picture.<br /><br />✔️<b>Using “YOUs”:</b> One thing I absolutely adore about this book is that the readers won’t feel left alone or read it as an outsider. The author sometimes tells the story including questions/explanations for us as if she’s making sure we’re on the same page with her. That’s really brilliant because the story sounds more like a diary this way and we’ll be able to feel closer to the characters.<br /><br />✔️<b>Bookworm Problems Alert!</b> Did I mention Charlie is also a booklover? She reads, fangirls, and dreams about being swept away by book boyfriends or jumping into the rabbit hole with Jase. Hence, <b>the fact</b> she reacts like most of us do (believe me, I know what you guys do secretly when you think no one’s watching) when it comes to books <b>reinforces the impression of the story.</b> This is another reason which makes me smile throughout the book, aside from her reveling in the sweet memory of being young.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I mean, come on, my best friend just asked me to kiss him with a quote from one of my favorite books!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Ending/Epilogue</b>
</u><br />Unfortunately, the epilogue is the only part I strongly dislike. I mean, the whole story is about a young girl’s life and I’d rather let her and her Prince Charming stay that way instead of zooming out to their life <b>50 frigging years later</b>! Although it’s still a HEA, the epilogue somehow feels foreign and out of place to me. I guess Christine Zolendz makes this arrangement because she wants to project the image of a once beautiful threesome (Charlie, Jase, Joey) again and wraps up the story beautifully. However, this feeling is too far away to grasp; hence, I would’ve enjoyed the book more if there were another ending or simply without the epilogue. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Though I do have an idea for a different ending: Perhaps Miss Zolendz could tell the readers more about Jase and Charlie’s life after they get back together and he embraces her regardless of the incident. I’m more interested in how or when they get married, have kids, or build a lovable family together. In my opinion, it’s a bit superficial to cover their 50-year-life-afterward in a few sentences such as “they live happily and everything’s perfect” or “their kids and grandchildren are doing fantastic and grow up healthily”; instead, I’d prefer more detailed information about their life together and how they deal with the loss and past. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />All in all, I’m truly, really, completely impressed with this story. The power of words, the courage those characters have, and the tremendous influence on me after reading it. There will never be enough words to describe my inner feelings when reading this book, so you’ll have to read it for yourself. Please give this book a try, guys. I’ll always be there when you need someone to talk to about the story. Lastly, <b><i>Here’s to Falling</i> is HIGHLY RECOMMENDED to everyone who wants your heart to be shattered by the strongest words I’ve ever read.</b> In other words, it’s a MUST-READ for you!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14550993797163382540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer15250028889017590854"><i>Here's <br/>to<br/>Falling.<br/>In love with one of the best books ever. </i><br/><br/>Holy freaking shit. I'm such a mess. This book...this book is not for the faint of the heart. It deals with so much tragedy and loss and heartbreak and lots of other shit that had me gasping, sobbing, praying for resolution and most of all, falling in love with these incredible characters. Jase, Charlie and Joey will reside in my heart for a very long time. I can barely see what I'm typing so I hope to God it makes sense. If not, well...o</span>
  <span id="freeText15250028889017590854" style="display:none"><i>Here's <br />to<br />Falling.<br />In love with one of the best books ever. </i><br /><br />Holy freaking shit. I'm such a mess. This book...this book is not for the faint of the heart. It deals with so much tragedy and loss and heartbreak and lots of other shit that had me gasping, sobbing, praying for resolution and most of all, falling in love with these incredible characters. Jase, Charlie and Joey will reside in my heart for a very long time. I can barely see what I'm typing so I hope to God it makes sense. If not, well...oh fucking well. I'm in physical pain from this journey but it was well worth the ride. Definitely recommend this book if you like crying your eyes out. Or stories that make you <i>feel </i>.<br /><br />I'll write a better review when I can get my bearings.</span>
