<div id="review_1260658266" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1260658266" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1260658266?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own-signed">pb-i-own-signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260658266" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10919788286499277907"><b><i>“It was you from the beginning … you were my horizon. Everything I could ever see.” </i><br/><br/>Stunning, emotional and an epically beautiful love story. <br/><br/>5 HUGE STARS</b><br/><br/>I read this book in one sitting. It’s now 2.30am and I can’t go to bed until I gush a bit because OMG, this book! The feels! Christine Zolendz has done an amazing job with this story – one based on true events which makes it even more meaningful. Both heartbreaking and tearfully beautiful, I absolutely loved it.<br/><br/>When we meet Charlie she is 24 ye</span>
  <span id="freeText10919788286499277907" style="display:none"><b><i>“It was you from the beginning … you were my horizon. Everything I could ever see.” </i><br /><br />Stunning, emotional and an epically beautiful love story. <br /><br />5 HUGE STARS</b><br /><br />I read this book in one sitting. It’s now 2.30am and I can’t go to bed until I gush a bit because OMG, this book! The feels! Christine Zolendz has done an amazing job with this story – one based on true events which makes it even more meaningful. Both heartbreaking and tearfully beautiful, I absolutely loved it.<br /><br />When we meet Charlie she is 24 years old, jaded and living under the tremendous burden of devastating memories from her past. She has been broken by the things that she has been through, but she carries on, and her strength is amazing.<br /><br /><blockquote><i>When I look back on all the past chapters of my life, I see all the pain I have endured. I see the mistakes and heartbreak, the horror and loss. But when I stand in front of the mirror now, I see all my scars and the strength I’ve found from them. I see the lessons I have learned about life and the wisdom I’ve gained from each of my experiences. </i>I will be fine.</blockquote><br />Charlie’s story is told in both the present and the past, with the story of the past intermingled with the present and unravelling slowly to show us all that happened to Charlie, and how she ended up where she is. She tells us the story of her past – growing up with her two best friends, Jase and Joey. The three of them had something incredibly special together, and the story of them growing up together is absolutely sensational! From sweet and innocent 9 year olds, through the awkward teen years, to senior high school, I loved every funny, sweet, cringe-worthy and heartbreaking moment of their time together as they shared absolutely everything and were there for each other through it all.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>Life knocks you down. It’s going to, and you got to just turn around and get back up, hold on to me if you have to, but always get back up. People will just walk all over you if you leave yourself beaten on the ground. </i>
</blockquote><br />The story is told primarily from Charlie’s perspective, but there are some other POV chapters in there which give the story a whole lot more depth. And as the story flicks back and forth between present and past, threads of the story are revealed, leaving you guessing what is happening and how it all fits together, and the way it’s woven together really draws you in. We are given hints about what is to come, and I read with a great sense of anticipation as it all came together. <br /><br />And, of course, there is a beautiful love story that is woven through both the past and the present. The beauty, wonder, and all-consuming nature of first love is brilliantly captured, only for it to be torn apart, creating the opportunity for a breath-taking, heart-pounding second chance romance. And with all that the characters go through, their love story takes on epic proportions as they battle against fate and the unfairness of life to find their way back to each other. <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“It was always you. Always. There is nothing you can tell me that will make me look at you as anything other than my Charlie.”<br /><br />“I want my best friend back. I want the best thing that ever happened to me back. And I promise you I will make you fall in love with me all over again. This time, it’ll be the forever kind.”</i>
</blockquote><br />There are a few storylines overlapping through the book, but don’t go looking for too many details before you make a start because you just need to dive in and experience it. But for those who need to know whether it has a happy ending or not… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes, it does. And it made me cry. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />And I must warn that it’s not an easy road for these characters and there are some really confronting scenes in this book that some readers may have issues with…. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ there is bullying, drug use, death, verbal abuse and physical and sexual assault – including a brutally graphic rape scene that is both horrifying and devastating <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I understand why Christine Zolendz told the story why she did, and as hard as those moments are to read, they convey an incredible depth of emotion, and help you relate to the characters, what they are going through, and the way they react to it all. It’s hard reading at times, and my heart broke over and over for all that these characters endure, but it just makes the happy times that much sweeter.<br /><br />I am a mad fan of all of Christine Zolendz’s books, and this book is no exception. She is a wonderful storyteller, combining romance and drama with light and funny moments, and she writes the best love stories – hot, passionate, and all-consuming, and she manages to infuse just the right amount of angst into it to make it incredibly intense and have me sitting on the edge of my seat with my hand held to my heart, tears streaming down my face and frantically flipping pages on my kindle. <br /><br />I absolutely loved this book!<br /><br />5 huge stars.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10919788286499277907" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1973904441?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1973904441" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12723238959367374189">5 stars<br/><br/>AMAZING childhood friends to lovers story! Their relationship spans over 15 years(from 9 year olds to 17 year olds, then separated for 7 years, only to meet again at 24) <br/>So gut wrenching and my heart broke so many times for this couple. <br/></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2480281585642216011">04/27/2015 --<br/><br/>Wow. That was tedious.<br/><br/>I read dedications. I wish I liked it more than I did.<br/><br/>Here's the deal .. I'm a very straightforward person. Why spend 10 words to say something when 2 will do as well.   <span id="freeText2480281585642216011" style="display:none">04/27/2015 --<br /><br />Wow. That was tedious.<br /><br />I read dedications. The dedication in this book gives you and idea that this is the story Ms. Zolendz was born to write. The story that feeds her and is her story. I wish I liked it more than I did.<br /><br />Here's the deal .. I'm a very straightforward person. Why spend 10 words to say something when 2 will do as well. Why try to paint a picture with words when those words lack feeling. This is what I got out of this book. You could tell she really tried. She tried to write flowery, thoughtful, thought provoking prose, but it just didn't work for me.<br /><br />She didn't pull me in. The story didn't suck me into it. I didn't care about the characters nor did I care about their situations. I couldn't imagine them. I didn't even get a good feel for the tree-house where so much of this story takes place.<br /><br />I found myself skimming parts of the book and even jumped a whole chapter just to finish it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When Joey died, I seriously didn't care. When Jase and Charlie found each other again -- I just wanted the darned thing to end. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I want to apologize to the author. I know this book is important to you and I hate that I didn't like it. I hope for you, I'm in the minority.<br /><br />I've tried one other book by this author and it didn't work for me either. I think my needs and her style are at an impasse so will avoid reading and reviewing more by her. I think that's fair.<br /><br />I'd give a more detailed review, but frankly, little worked for me here, so won't bore you.<br /><br />Happy [maybe] Reading!<br /><br /><b>+++++++++++++++++++++++++++<br />Overall Rating = 2 Stars<br />Book Cover / Book Blurb / Book Title = 3 / 5 / 3 = 3.5 Stars<br />Writer’s Voice = 2 Stars<br />Character / Secondary Character Development = 3 / 3 = 3 Stars<br />“Did I like” Hero / Heroine = 3 / 1 = 2 Stars<br />Story / Background Story Development = 2 / 2 = 2 Stars<br />“Did I like the Damned Thing” = 1.5 Stars<br />Ending = 3 Stars<br />Worth the Chili = 2 Stars -- [$2.99 on Amazon]<br />Smexy [HEAT] Rating = Mild<br />259 pages<br /></b><br /><i>First sentence: It was the edge of forever ago.<br /><br />Last sentence: I miss the shit out of you. </i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7358022181254602890">This was probably one of the most emotional reads for me this year. I loved the author’s style of storytelling, I’m pretty certain it must have been really difficult for her to write this story, some emotional scars developed along the way. This sort of writing commitment just really inspires me as a reader and I salute her for bringing to life such a beautifully written story which required her to really step in to the main characters shoes.<br/><br/>This was a beautiful story about friendship, loss, ove</span>
  <span id="freeText7358022181254602890" style="display:none">This was probably one of the most emotional reads for me this year. I loved the author’s style of storytelling, I’m pretty certain it must have been really difficult for her to write this story, some emotional scars developed along the way. This sort of writing commitment just really inspires me as a reader and I salute her for bringing to life such a beautifully written story which required her to really step in to the main characters shoes.<br><br>This was a beautiful story about friendship, loss, overcoming that loss and trying to survive the tribulations of life. This is real life guys, surviving. I just think the characters were really well written, it was brought to life in a fantastic way and honestly, these characters will stay with you forever. As will this story. I recommend this to everybody. Sorry I do not have the heart to speak much about this. It’s just beautiful. And don’t worry there is most definitely a happy ending! But it just catches your heart.<br><br>The story is also told through flashbacks so you’re constantly second guessing certain things in the present which may have been caused by the past. It certainly keeps you entertained from beginning to end. No doubt a must read!<br><br>Ps. If I could re-do my list of top 10 reads of 2015, this would most definitely be included!<br><br><i>
  <b>My flesh only felt alive where his fingertips touched down; the rest of my body was just shadows and memories of us.</b>

<div id="review_1253885052" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1253885052" />
    <a title="Judy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17677483-judy"><img alt="Judy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410903662p2/17677483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1253885052?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Judy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Judy" href="/user/show/17677483-judy">Judy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17677483-judy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17677483-judy?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17677483-judy?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17677483-judy?shelf=arc-or-beta">arc-or-beta</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1253885052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5741342011713944077">Friends, love, inspired by true events ...... how can you not read this? You must. And you must have tissues available! That is my warning to you!<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>'I've heard some people say that what you remember is not the whole truth; it's our thoughts of what we wanted things to be remembered as. They believe that we change our memories, that we just fabricate them into pasts that we can live with.<br/>Do I believe that?<br/>No. I believe I remember, every little detail."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>This is the story of three friends, that sp</span>
  <span id="freeText5741342011713944077" style="display:none">Friends, love, inspired by true events ...... how can you not read this? You must. And you must have tissues available! That is my warning to you!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>'I've heard some people say that what you remember is not the whole truth; it's our thoughts of what we wanted things to be remembered as. They believe that we change our memories, that we just fabricate them into pasts that we can live with.<br>Do I believe that?<br>No. I believe I remember, every little detail."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is the story of three friends, that spans across a fifteen year period taking you to both the past and present. I'll admit, I'm not usually a big fan of that, but this flowed smoothly between the two and I loved every minute of it.<br><br>Heroine:<br>Charlotte (Charlie) is a spunky, quirky little girl who wears glasses and loves to read. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"thou shalt not bother me until I finished thy chapter"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Eventually Charlie grows up.....<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Was the grass greener someplace else, or was it fertilized with loads of bullshit like it was on my side?"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Hero:<br>There are two, Joey and Jase. And they are heroes in every sense of the word.<br>One boy has soft sweet brown eyes, while the other has piercing blues unlike anything you've ever seen.<br><br>As kids these three had me laughing out loud. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"the kids stuck up his middle finger at me"</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"It means he hates you and wants to poke you in the eye really hard with his finger. Duh."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>But as the story goes on, the laughing turned to tears. Sometimes of joy, and sometimes.... well.... not.<br>This is their journey of discovery, friendship, strength, tragedy, loss, and love. These three have an unbreakable bond and it was beautiful to read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429053796i/14523292.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This isn't a 'dark read', nor is it purely an 'emotionally draining' read. It has both of those elements, yes, don't get me wrong, there's some terrible things that will have you gasping and cringing, but it's also incredibly sweet and funny, and there's also an easy going feel at times, mixed with a bit of mystery. I knew there was something I was missing, something had to have happened and when it was revealed, I was crushed. Hence the tissue warning. In the back of my mind I thought to myself, was this the part that happened in real life? I read on, I wiped my tears, I laughed again, I was happy, I loved these characters and their quirkiness, then I was crying again. Is this the part? I was devastated.<br><br><br>These characters are beautiful, this story is inspirational and I implore you to read it! Go on... go down the rabbit hole with Charlie, Jase and Joey!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1429053796i/14523291._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*I received an arc from the author for an honest review<br><br><br><a href="http://judys-confessions.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read more at Judy's Confessions</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5741342011713944077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1256206428?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="1-Click Addict Support Group" class="user" itemprop="url" name="1-Click Addict Support Group" href="/user/show/22365152-1-click-addict-support-group">1-Click Addict Support Group</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1256206428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16931858018528773473">God damn, I need wine <i>stat</i> after finishing this book. I'm not talking about a glass or a bottle either, I'm talking a big ole five liter box of wine. And maybe throw in some Xanax for good measure. <i>Here's to Falling</i> is one of those epic sagas of childhood friendship turned to love. You know that saying, "I need therapy because of books," or something along those lines? That. Is. This. Book.<br/><br/>I laughed, I cried heaving sobs, I had my heart broken, all of it at the hands of this story. This is beaut</span>
  <span id="freeText16931858018528773473" style="display:none">God damn, I need wine <i>stat</i> after finishing this book. I'm not talking about a glass or a bottle either, I'm talking a big ole five liter box of wine. And maybe throw in some Xanax for good measure. <i>Here's to Falling</i> is one of those epic sagas of childhood friendship turned to love. You know that saying, "I need therapy because of books," or something along those lines? That. Is. This. Book.<br /><br />I laughed, I cried heaving sobs, I had my heart broken, all of it at the hands of this story. This is beautiful and emotional. It does deal with some very tough, graphic subject matter, so be warned. The fact that Christine lived through some of these events and laid herself bare to her readers really struck a chord with me. I applaud her for her courage to put this book out there into the reading community.<br /><br />Honestly, I don't think I can even write up a summary for <i>Here's to Falling</i>. There is so much that happens in this book you just need to read it for yourself. It's a book that's going to stay with me for a long time and I kinda feel sorry for the book I have to read next for review; this one is going to be a hard act to follow. ~ Erin, 6 stars </span>
  <a data-text-id="16931858018528773473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13274540938899564655">4.25 stars!<br/><br/>Books based on true experiences always attract me. At the beginning where author wrote it's based on her true story, I was mesmerized into it. At some parts story dragged a little bit, but I understand author wrote it mainly because of herself, reader was not main focus in this story. If you read it carefully, you can notice where she added some parts to make it a "story". <br/>I really appreciate when authors are willing to share their true stories, no matter how painful they are.<br/><br/><br/></span>

  <span id="freeText6711669986848215795" style="display:none">5 If I could give it a million stars<br><br>First and foremost WOW!!!!!<br><br>OMFG, yes I'm writing it in shouty letters because OMFG, I FLOVED this book so Hard. <br><br>Nothing I say or write will express how fantastic this book is. In the hours it took me to read this beautiful masterpiece, I had my heart broken a thousand times. I ugly cried HUGE, I smiled like a kid on Christmas morning, my head was booming by the end and I was once again reminded that life is far too short. <br><br>At the very beginning of this book we learn that parts of the story are based on real life, I honesty think that, that one sentence, added massively to my emotions and reactions because let me tell you, I was a tear stained, wine guzzling mess. Christine Zolendz, I solute you, you knocked this one right out of the park. <br><br>I seriously don't want to give anything away, I can't possibly break this down, the synopsis is very brief for a reason and going in blind only increases the impact of heartbreak and unconditional love within these pages. <br><br>The characters were beyond perfect, the writing was spectacular and above all else, it felt so different from anything I've ever read before. <br><br><a href="http://s1368.photobucket.com/user/salomax1/media/164f535521c039f1339d07e015787152_zpsulytlp9p.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1245801655" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9501896-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513212035p2/9501896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1245801655?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/9501896-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1245801655" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1874368600935561173">Within the first few lines of Here's to Falling, I was hooked. <br/><br/>I fell. Hard. Loved it and couldn't put it down. <br/><br/>I love all of Christine Zolendz's books, so when I read the blurb for this one, I couldn't wait to get my hands on it. This is a story of three best friends who have an incredible bond. We see them grow together, doing all the crazy things best friends do. Joey, Jase, and Charlie. Inseparable. I loved hearing all about their childhood adventures and watching them go through high school</span>
  <span id="freeText1874368600935561173" style="display:none">Within the first few lines of Here's to Falling, I was hooked. <br /><br />I fell. Hard. Loved it and couldn't put it down. <br /><br />I love all of Christine Zolendz's books, so when I read the blurb for this one, I couldn't wait to get my hands on it. This is a story of three best friends who have an incredible bond. We see them grow together, doing all the crazy things best friends do. Joey, Jase, and Charlie. Inseparable. I loved hearing all about their childhood adventures and watching them go through high school together. Christine's writing is perfect, you feel as if you're right there with them through all the trials and tribulations they faced while growing up.<br /><br />The emotions I felt while reading were just all over the place. I laughed, I cried, but most of all I fell in love. Each character was perfectly crafted, strong in their own way. I didn't love one more than another.<br /><br />This is a love story of the truest form. It's a story of first love, true love, never-ending love. <br /><br />"Here's to falling... in love...and to the best example of it that I've ever seen, which is sitting right in front of me."<br /><br />I'm not going to tell you anything about the story. Go in blind with just the synopsis in your head. There were so many holy sh*t moments that I had to stop to take a breath. Christine nailed it!! I didn't want it to end. I was blown away. If I could give this one more than 5 stars I would. So I am. This was a huge BOOKGASM for me. Loved, loved, loved it!!! 6+++++++ Stars! Go one click!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1874368600935561173" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zb2G78qoTrK8dpHv56f8+wJNNH9EB09bSuDySpSzeCv8MjZeITCdFIidoQnCNvEZUN13Kdxj1Wa0AlmlBNtIzQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HWMO9aSTFoM95vzz1ihAt1DNOD9uWxahd+bdwtTv2k4s7L5ETwvFJQkNzBXzuU1VAl17afY/jJyJBHYtRIfqqA==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/45021446-here-s-to-falling">Quotes from Here&#39;s to Falling</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Life knocks you down. It’s going to, and you got to just turn around and get back up, hold on to me if you have to, but always get back up. People will just walk all over you if you leave yourself beaten on the ground.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/6938975-life-knocks-you-down-it-s-going-to-and-you-got">12 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Here’s the twist to your story, Charlie. You ready for it?" he growled and nipped at my lower lip. "Breathe me in deep. Hold your breath. I will make you fall in love with me again. Because I sure as shit didn’t think I’d ever see you again, and I sure as shit didn’t think I could fall in love with you again, but I did." His hands gripped me tighter. "Like I was falling from a cliff, Charlie. Then...then…I realized when I hit the ground; I’ve been in love with you this whole time. It never stopped. I’ll never stop. I will never stop, and I will never give up on you." His voice lowered, “It was you from the beginning, the minute you taped that skull and crossbones to your window wearing those baggy jeans, that Nirvana T-shirt, and those God-awful chucks, you were my horizon. Everything I could ever see.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/6881256-here-s-the-twist-to-your-story-charlie-you-ready-for">11 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
        <a class="actionLink" style="float: right" href="/work/quotes/45021446-here-s-to-falling">More quotes&hellip;</a>
